'' : v).toLowerCase() === 'true' || v === true || v === '是' || v === 'yes' || v === 'TRUE' || v === '1'; } function compatTextBool_(v) { return compatBool_(v) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE'; } function parseTimeString_(v) { var s = sanitize_(v || ''); if (!s) return ''; var m = s.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})/); if (m) return ('0' + m[1]).slice(-2) + ':' + m[2]; var d = new Date(s); if (String(d) !== 'Invalid Date') return Utilities.formatDate(d, TIMEZONE, 'HH:mm'); return s; } function timeStringToMinutes_(v) { var s = parseTimeString_(v); if (!/^\d{2}:\d{2}$/.test(s)) return NaN; return Number(s.slice(0,2)) * 60 + Number(s.slice(3,5)); } function minutesToTimeString_(n) { var h = Math.floor(n / 60); var m = n % 60; return ('0' + h).slice(-2) + ':' + ('0' + m).slice(-2); } function computeRestBreaksByShift_(startTime, endTime) { var start = timeStringToMinutes_(startTime); var end = timeStringToMinutes_(endTime); if (isNaN(start) || isNaN(end) || end <= start) return []; var breaks = []; var threshold = start + 240; while (threshold < end) { var breakEnd = Math.min(threshold + 30, end); if (breakEnd > threshold) breaks.push({ start: minutesToTimeString_(threshold), end: minutesToTimeString_(breakEnd) }); threshold += 270; } return breaks; } function dateKeyToDate_(key) { var s = sanitize_(key); ['標準打卡','特殊打卡'] : ['標準打卡'] }; } function clockSheetMeta_() { var headers = ['紀錄ID','員工ID','姓名','Email','打卡日期','打卡時間','打卡動作','打卡方式','狀態','遲到分鐘','備註','來源IP','是否補登','原始紀錄ID','建立時間','最後更新時間']; var sh = ensureSheet_(SHEETS.clock, headers); ensureHeaders_(sh, headers); var meta = headerMap_(sh); return { sh: sh, headers: meta.headers, map: meta.map }; } function clockFailSheetMeta_() { var headers = ['失敗ID','員工ID','姓名','Email','打卡動作','打卡方式','來源IP','失敗原因','建立時間']; var sh = ensureSheet_(SHEETS.clockFail, headers); ensureHeaders_(sh, headers); var meta = headerMap_(sh); return { sh: sh, headers: meta.headers, map: meta.map }; } function monthlyReportLogSheetMeta_() { var headers = ['寄送ID','員工ID','姓名','Email','月份','打卡筆數','附件檔名','寄送狀態','訊息','建立時間']; var sh = ensureSheet_(SHEETS.monthlyReportLog, headers); ensureHeaders_(sh, headers); var meta = headerMap_(sh); return { sh: sh, headers: meta.headers, map: meta.map }; } function clockCorrectionSheetMeta_() { var headers = ['申請ID','員工ID','姓名','Email','原始紀錄ID','修正日期','修正時間','修正動作','修正打卡方式','修正原因','狀態','審核時間','審核人員ID','審核人員姓名','駁回理由','建立時間','最後更新時間','核准後紀錄ID']; var sh = ensureSheet_(SHEETS.clockCorrections, headers); ensureHeaders_(sh, headers); var meta = headerMap_(sh); return { sh: sh, headers: meta.headers, map: meta.map }; } function clockCorrectionPageUrl_() { var pageUrl = settingsPageUrl_(); return pageUrl ? var sh = ensureSheet_(SHEETS.parttime, headers); ensureHeaders_(sh, headers); var meta = headerMap_(sh); return { sh: sh, headers: meta.headers, map: meta.map }; } function parttimeNormalizeHoursValue_(value) { if (value == null || value === '') return 0; if (typeof value === 'number') { if (!isFinite(value) || value < 0 || value > 24) return 0; return Math.round(value * 100) / 100; } if (Object.prototype.toString.call(value) === '[object Date]' && !isNaN(value.getTime())) { var ref = new Date(1899, 11, 30, 0, 0, 0, 0); var diffHours = (value.getTime() - ref.getTime()) / 3600000; if (isFinite(diffHours) && diffHours >= 0 && diffHours <= 24) { return Math.round(diffHours * 100) / 100; } return 0; } var raw = sanitize_(value).replace(/小時/g, '').replace(/hours?/ig, '').replace(/hr/ig, '').trim(); if (!raw) return 0; if (/^\d{1,2}:\d{2}(:\d{2})?$/.test(raw)) { var parts = raw.split(':'); var hh = Number(parts[0] || 0) || 0; var mm = Number(parts[1] || 0) || 0; var ss = Number(parts[2] || 0) || 0; var timeHours = hh + (mm / 60) + (ss / 3600); if (timeHours >= 0 && timeHours <= 24) return Math.round(timeHours * 100) / 100; return 0; } var matched = raw.match(/-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?/); if (!matched) return 0; var num = Number(matched[0] || 0) || 0; if (!isFinite(num) || num < 0 || num > 24) return 0; return Math.round(num * 100) / 100; } function parttimeEmployeePayrollSnapshot_(empObj) { var cfg = employeeSalaryConfigFromRow_(empObj || {}); } function parttimeExpectedEntryStatus_(workDate, endTime) { var target = sanitize_(workDate || ''); var today = todayKey_(); if (!target) return '正常'; if (compareDateKey_(target, today) < 0) return '補時數'; var meta = announcementSheetMetaCompat_(); var rowIndex = findRowByValue_(meta.sh, meta.map['公告ID'] + 1, sanitize_(data.announcementId || data.id)); if (!rowIndex) return { ok: false, message: '找不到公告。' }; meta.sh.deleteRow(rowIndex); return { ok: true, message: '公告已刪除。' }; } function toggleAnnouncement_(data) { requireAdminByUserId_(data.userId || findFirstAdminId_()); var meta = announcementSheetMetaCompat_();
